year">common year</a> <a href="/wiki/Common_year_starting_on_Thursday" title="Common year starting on Thursday">starting on Thursday</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Gregorian_calendar" title="Gregorian calendar">Gregorian calendar</a>, the 2015th year of the <a href="/wiki/Common_Era" title="Common Era">Common Era</a> (CE) and <i><a href="/wiki/Anno_Domini" title="Anno Domini">Anno Domini</a></i> (AD) designations, the 15th  year of the <a href="/wiki/3rd_millennium" title="3rd millennium">3rd&#160;millennium</a>, the 15th  year of the <a href="/wiki/21st_century" title="21st century">21st&#160;century</a>, and the  6th   year of the <a href="/wiki/2010s" title="2010s">2010s</a> decade.\n</p>\n<table class="infobox" width="300">\n\n<tbody><tr>\n<td class="toclevel-1 tocsection-31"><a href="#References"><span class="tocnumber">7</span> <span class="toctext">References</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p><br />\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Events">Events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2015&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January">January</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2015&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: January">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/January_1" title="January 1">January 1</a>\n<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Eurasian_Economic_Union" title="Eurasian Economic Union">Eurasian Economic Union</a> comes into effect, creating a <a href="/wiki/Political_union" title="Political union">political</a> and <a href="/wiki/Economic_union" title="Economic union">economic union</a> between <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Armenia" title="Armenia">Armenia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan" title="Kazakhstan">Kazakhstan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kyrgyzstan" title="Kyrgyzstan">Kyrgyzstan</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Lithuania" title="Lithuania">Lithuania</a> officially <a href="/wiki/Lithuania_and_the_euro" title="Lithuania and the euro">adopts</a> the <a href="/wiki/Euro" title="Euro">euro</a> as its currency, replacing the <a href="/wiki/Lithuanian_litas" title="Lithuanian litas">litas</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Enlargement_of_the_eurozone" title="Enlargement of the eurozone">becomes</a> the nineteenth <a href="/wiki/Eurozone" title="Eurozone">Eurozone</a> country.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/January_3" title="January 3">January 3</a>&#8211;<a href="/wiki/January_7" title="January 7">7</a> &#8211; A <a href="/wiki/2015_Baga_massacre" title="2015 Baga massacre">series of massacres in Baga</a>, Nigeria and surrounding villages by <a href="/wiki/Boko_Haram" title="Boko Haram">Boko Haram</a> kills more than 2,000 people.<sup id="cite_ref-AFP_BI_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AFP_BI-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBC_1_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_1-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-NBC_News_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NBC_News-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Reuters_1_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Reuters_1-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/January_7" title="January 7">January 7</a> \xe2\x80\x93 Two gunmen belonging to <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda_in_the_Arabian_Peninsula" title="Al-Qaeda in the Arabian Peninsula">Al-Qaeda</a>\'s <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a> branch <a href="/wiki/Charlie_Hebdo_shooting" title="Charlie Hebdo shooting">kill 12 people and injure 11 more</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> headquarters of satirical newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/Charlie_Hebdo" title="Charlie Hebdo">Charlie Hebdo</a></i>, prompting an anti-terrorism demonstration attended by over a million people and more than 40 world leaders.<sup id="cite_ref-BreedenCharlieHebdo_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BreedenCharlieHebdo-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AldermanBilefskyCharlieHebdo_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AldermanBilefskyCharlieHebdo-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/January_12" title="January 12">January 12</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/January_2015_raid_on_Kolofata" title="January 2015 raid on Kolofata">Government raids</a> kill 143 Boko Haram fighters in Kolofata, Cameroon.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/January_15" title="January 15">January 15</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Swiss_National_Bank" title="Swiss National Bank">Swiss National Bank</a> abandons the cap on the <a href="/wiki/Swiss_franc" title="Swiss franc">franc</a>\'s value relative to the <a href="/wiki/Euro" title="Euro">euro</a>, causing turmoil in international financial markets.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a The ancient city sites of <a href="/wiki/Nimrud" title="Nimrud">Nimrud</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hatra" title="Hatra">Hatra</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dur-Sharrukin" title="Dur-Sharrukin">Dur-Sharrukin</a> in Iraq are demolished by the <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/March_6" title="March 6">March 6</a> &#8211; A <a href="/wiki/2015_Bangkok_bombing" title="2015 Bangkok bombing">bombing</a> takes place inside the <a href="/wiki/Erawan_Shrine" title="Erawan Shrine">Erawan Shrine</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Ratchaprasong" title="Ratchaprasong">Ratchaprasong</a> intersection in <a href="/wiki/Pathum_Wan_District" title="Pathum Wan District">Pathum Wan District</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bangkok,_Thailand" class="mw-redirect" title="Bangkok, Thailand">Bangkok, Thailand</a>, killing 20 people and injuring 125.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="September">September</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2015&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: September">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/September_10" title="September 10">September 10</a> &#8211; Scientists announce the discovery of <i><a href="/wiki/Homo_naledi" title="Homo naledi">Homo naledi</a></i>, a previously unknown species of <a href="/wiki/Homo" title="Homo">early human</a> in <a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South Africa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/September_11" title="September 11">September 11</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Queen_Elizabeth_II" class="mw-redirect" title="Queen Elizabeth II">Queen Elizabeth II</a>, having been on the throne for 63&#160;years, 217&#160;days, became the longest-reigning British monarch in history and the longest-serving head of state of any nation in modern history, surpassing <a href="/wiki/Queen_Victoria" title="Queen Victoria">Queen Victoria</a> who had reigned for 63&#160;years, 216&#160;days upon her death on January 22, 1901.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/September_14" title="September 14">September 14</a>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/First_observation_of_gravitational_waves" title="First observation of gravitational waves">First observation of gravitational waves</a>: <a href="/wiki/Gravitational_wave" title="Gravitational wave">Gravitational waves</a> are detected for the first time, by <a href="/wiki/LIGO" title="LIGO">LIGO</a>. This is not announced until February 11, 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Malcolm_Turnbull" title="Malcolm Turnbull">Malcolm Turnbull</a> defeats <a href="/wiki/Tony_Abbott" title="Tony Abbott">Tony Abbott</a> in a <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Party_of_Australia" title="Liberal Party of Australia">Liberal Party</a> <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Party_of_Australia_leadership_spill,_September_2015" title="Liberal Party of Australia leadership spill, September 2015">leadership ballot</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Turnbull becomes <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Australia" title="Prime Minister of Australia">Prime Minister of Australia</a>, being sworn in the following day.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/September_18" title="September 18">September 18</a> &#8211; Automaker <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen" title="Volkswagen">Volkswagen</a> is alleged to have been involved in worldwide <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_emissions_scandal" title="Volkswagen emissions scandal">rigging of diesel emissions tests</a>, affecting an estimated 11 million vehicles globally.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/September_24" title="September 24">September 24</a> &#8211; A <a href="/wiki/2015_Mina_stampede" title="2015 Mina stampede">stampede</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Hajj" title="Hajj">Hajj</a> pilgrimage in <a href="/wiki/Mecca" title="Mecca">Mecca</a> kills at least 2,200 people and injures more than 900 others, with more than 650 missing.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/September_28" title="September 28">September 28</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a> announces that liquid water has been found on <a href="/wiki/Mars" title="Mars">Mars</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/September_30" title="September 30">September 30</a> &#8211; Russia begins <a href="/wiki/Russian_military_intervention_in_Syria" class="mw-redirect" title="Russian military intervention in Syria">air strikes</a> against <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a> and <a href="/wiki/Syrian_opposition" title="Syrian opposition">anti-government forces</a> in Syria, in support of the Syrian government.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October">October</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2015&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: October">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/October_3" title="October 3">October 3</a> &#8211; A <a href="/wiki/Kunduz_hospital_airstrike" title="Kunduz hospital airstrike">United States airstrike</a> on a <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A9decins_Sans_Fronti%C3%A8res" title="M\xc3\xa9decins Sans Fronti\xc3\xa8res">M\xc3\xa9decins Sans Fronti\xc3\xa8res</a> (Doctors Without Borders) hospital in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> accidentally kills an estimated 20 people.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/October_10" title="October 10">October 10</a> &#8211; A series of <a href="/wiki/2015_Ankara_bombings" title="2015 Ankara bombings">suicide bombings</a> kills at least 100 people at a peace rally in <a href="/wiki/Ankara,_Turkey" class="mw-redirect" title="Ankara, Turkey">Ankara, Turkey</a>, and injures more than 400 others.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/October_23" title="October 23">October 23</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Patricia" title="Hurricane Patricia">Hurricane Patricia</a> becomes the most <a href="/wiki/List_of_tropical_cyclone_records" title="List of tropical cyclone records">intense</a> hurricane ever recorded in the <a href="/wiki/Western_Hemisphere" title="Western Hemisphere">Western Hemisphere</a> and the second strongest worldwide, with winds of 215&#160;mph and a pressure of 872 mbar.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/October_26" title="October 26">October 26</a> &#8211; A <a href="/wiki/2015_Hindu_Kush_earthquake" class="mw-redirect" title="2015 Hindu Kush earthquake">magnitude 7.5 earthquake</a> strikes the <a href="/wiki/Hindu_Kush" title="Hindu Kush">Hindu Kush</a> region and causes 398 deaths,<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> with 279 in <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>, 115 in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> and 4 in <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/October_31" title="October 31">October 31</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Kogalymavia_Flight_9268" class="mw-redirect" title="Kogalymavia Flight 9268">Kogalymavia Flight 9268</a>, an <a href="/wiki/Airbus_A321" title="Airbus A321">Airbus A321</a> airliner en route to <a href="/wiki/Saint_Petersburg" title="Saint Petersburg">Saint Petersburg</a> from <a href="/wiki/Sharm_el-Sheikh" class="mw-redirect" title="Sharm el-Sheikh">Sharm el-Sheikh</a>, crashes near Al-Hasana in Sinai, killing all 217 passengers and 7 crew members on board.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="November">November</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2015&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: November">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/November_7" title="November 7">November 7</a> &#8211; Chinese and Taiwanese presidents, <a href="/wiki/Xi_Jinping" title="Xi Jinping">Xi Jinping</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ma_Ying-jeou" title="Ma Ying-jeou">Ma Ying-jeou</a>, <a href="/wiki/2015_Ma%E2%80%93Xi_meeting" class="mw-redirect" title="2015 Ma\xe2\x80\x93Xi meeting">formally meet</a> for the first time.<sup id="cite_ref-cnaupdate_68-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cnaupdate-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/November_12" title="November 12">November 12</a> &#8211; Two suicide bombers <a href="/wiki/2015_Beirut_bombings" title="2015 Beirut bombings">detonated explosives</a> in Bourj el-Barajneh, Beirut, killing 43 people and injuring over 200 others.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/November_13" title="November 13">November 13</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/November_2015_Paris_attacks" title="November 2015 Paris attacks">Multiple terrorist attacks</a> claimed by <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant</a> (ISIL) in <a href="/wiki/Paris,_France" class="mw-redirect" title="Paris, France">Paris, France</a>, result in 130 fatalities.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/November_24" title="November 24">November 24</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> <a href="/wiki/2015_Russian_Sukhoi_Su-24_shootdown" title="2015 Russian Sukhoi Su-24 shootdown">shoots down</a> a <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> fighter jet on the <a href="/wiki/Syria%E2%80%93Turkey_border" title="Syria\xe2\x80\x93Turkey border">Turkish-Syrian border</a> in the first case of a <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> member destroying a Russian aircraft since the 1950s.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/November_30" title="November 30">November 30</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/2015_United_Nations_Climate_Change_Conference" title="2015 United Nations Climate Change Conference">2015 United Nations Climate Change Conference</a> (COP 21) is held in Paris, attended by leaders from 147 nations.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="December">December</span><span time.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/December_15" title="December 15">December 15</a> &#8211; The <a class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/December_22" title="December 22">December 22</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/SpaceX" title="SpaceX">SpaceX</a> lands an unmanned <a href="/wiki/Falcon_9" title="Falcon 9">Falcon 9</a> rocket, the first <a href="/wiki/Reusable_launch_system" title="Reusable launch system">reusable rocket</a> to successfully enter orbital space and return.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Births">Births</span><span
